017596,003109:    4216                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
017597,003110:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
017598,003111:    4216           35010        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #     THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
017599,003112:    4217           55022                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
017600,003113:                                                                                                  #   MONITOR BIT.
017601,003114:    4220           00002                           TC       Q                                     
017602,003115: 
017603,003116: 
017604,003117:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT  +0 INACTIVE(WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
017605,003118:                                                                                                  #            +1  PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
017606,003119:                                                                                                  #           -1 TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
017607,003120:                                                                                                  #           -0    DATA IN      SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
017608,003121:                                                                                                  #              OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
017609,003122: 
017610,003123: 
017611,003124:                                                                                                  #  L  TC ENDIDLE  (FIXED FIXED)
017612,003125:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
017613,003126:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
017614,003127:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
017615,003128:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
017616,003129:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
017617,003130:                                                                                                  #  L+1      FOR TERMINATE
017618,003131:                                                                                                  #  L+2      FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
017619,003132:                                                                                                  #  L+3      FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
017620,003133:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
017621,003134: 
017622,003135: 
017623,003136:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
017624,003137:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
017625,003138:                                                                                                  #  1) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
017626,003139:                                                                                                  #  EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
017627,003140:                                                                                                  #  2) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
017628,003141:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY.
017629,003142: 
017630,003143:    4221           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
017631,003144:    4222           04232                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
017632,003145:    4223           04236                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
017633,003146:    4224           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
017634,003147:    4225           75062                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
017635,003148:    4226           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
017636,003149:    4227           55043                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
017637,003150:    4230           05203                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
017638,003151: 
017639,003152: 
017640,003153:    4231           05225        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB

017982,003495:    4450           00002                           TC       Q                                     
017983,003496: 
017984,003497:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
017985,003498: 
017986,003499:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
017987,003500:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
017988,003501:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
017989,003502:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
017990,003503: 
017991,003504:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
017992,003505:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
017993,003506:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
017994,003507:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
017995,003508:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
017996,003509:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
017997,003510:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
017998,003511: 
017999,003512: 
018000,003513:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
018001,003514:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
018002,003515:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
018003,003516:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
018004,003517:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
018005,003518: 
018006,003519: 
018007,003520:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
018008,003521:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
018009,003522:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
018010,003523:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
018011,003524:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
018012,003525: 
018013,003526: 
018014,003527:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
018015,003528:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
018016,003529:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
018017,003530: 
018018,003531: 
018019,003532:                                                                                                  #  .
018020,003533: 
018021,003534: 
018022,003535:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
018023,003536:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
018024,003537:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
018025,003538:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
018026,003539: 
018027,003540: 
018028,003541:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
018029,003542:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
018030,003543:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
018031,003544:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
018032,003545:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
018033,003546:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING
018034,003547:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
018035,003548: 
018036,003549:    4451           44456        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
018037,003550:    4452           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF(LOC
018038,003551:    4453           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
018039,003552:    4454           04674        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
018040,003553:    4455           10521                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
018041,003554:    4456           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
018042,003555: 
018043,003556:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
018044,003557:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
018045,003558: 
018046,003559: 04,2521                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
018047,003560: 04,2521                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
018048,003561: 04,2521           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
018049,003562: 04,2522           04232                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
018050,003563: 04,2523           04236                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
018051,003564: 04,2524           04406                           TC       RELDSPON                              
018052,003565: 04,2525           30001                           CA       L                                     
018053,003566: 04,2526           55044                           TS       DSPLIST                               
018054,003567: 04,2527           05203        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
018055,003568: 
018056,003569: 
018057,003570:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
018058,003571:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
018059,003572:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
018060,003573:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
018061,003574:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
018062,003575: 
018063,003576:    4457                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
018064,003577:    4457                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
018065,003578:    4457           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
018066,003579:    4460           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
018067,003580:    4461           35011                           CAF      BIT14                                 
018068,003581:    4462           71022                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
018069,003582:    4463           61013                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
018070,003583:    4464           10000                           CCS      A                                     
018071,003584:    4465           14467                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
018072,003585:    4466           14176                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
018073,003586:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
018074,003587:    4467           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
018075,003588:    4470           14451                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
018076,003589: 
018077,003590: 
018078,003591:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
018079,003592:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
018080,003593:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
018081,003594:    4471           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
018082,003595:    4472           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
018083,003596:    4473           45011                           CS       BIT14                                 
018084,003597:    4474           00004                           INHINT                                         
018085,003598:    4475           71022                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
018086,003599:    4476           55022                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
018087,003600:    4477           11044                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
018088,003601:    4500           04502                           TC       +2                                    
018089,003602:    4501           04505                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
018090,003603:    4502           35030                           CAF      ZERO                                  
018091,003604:    4503           57044                           XCH      DSPLIST                               
018092,003605:    4504           05207                           TC       JOBWAKE                               
018093,003606:    4505           00003        RELDSP2            RELINT                                         
018094,003607:    4506           45022                           CS       BIT5                                  #  TURN OFF KEY RELEASE LIGHT
018095,003608:    4507           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11)
018096,003609:    4510           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              
018097,003610:    4511           35030                           CAF      ZERO                                  
018098,003611:    4512           55013                           TS       DSPLOCK
